News Highlights

The Case of Jiang Zhihuan's Surrender of Rights and Humiliation of the Nation 31

The Control Yuan Announces the Process of Impeachment

The case of Zhuang Zhihuan, the former Director of the Department of Electrical Affairs of the Ministry of Communications, who revised the underwater cable contracts of the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific companies, thereby surrendering rights and humiliating the nation, has been brought forward for impeachment by the Control Yuan, and the handling process has been announced. The details are recorded as follows:

Full Text of the Impeachment: Control Yuan members Tian Jiongjin, Gao Yihan, Liu Eqing, and others submitted an impeachment document against Zhuang Zhihuan, Director of the Department of Electrical Affairs of the Ministry of Communications, stating: "It is submitted that Zhuang Zhihuan, Director of the Department of Electrical Affairs of the Ministry of Communications, negotiated with the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and other companies regarding international telecommunications submarine cables. The conditions agreed upon violated the Party's foreign policy and the policy of independent electrical recognition, as well as the solutions proposed by the Ministry of Communications, constituting dereliction of duty and surrender of rights. It is appropriate to immediately bring forward an impeachment. We believe that the Party's political program and government policies are based on the principle of recovering national sovereignty and freedom of international communication. It has been investigated that on January 1, Year 19, the Executive Yuan forwarded a document to the National Government, stating that, according to the joint report of the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Communications, no government, company, or individual of any country will be granted exclusive rights to land submarine cables within Chinese territory. Furthermore, it has been investigated that on May 18, Year 18, the Executive Yuan secretly submitted a document to the National Government, stating that the Ministry of Communications proposed a comprehensive solution for the Great Eastern and Great Northern companies: (D) All patent privilege contracts and other contracts containing clauses regarding patent privileges should be notified for cancellation immediately. (E) The Ministry of Communications should notify the two companies that the landing and connection contracts can be maintained until 1930, i.e., the end of the 19th year of the Republic. All submarine cables installed within Chinese territorial waters shall be owned by China and taken over by the Ministry of Communications of the National Government. In the event that negotiations result in the cables still needing to be managed by the companies after 1930, and the right to land and connect cannot be cancelled, then the following conditions are the minimum requirements and must be acknowledged by the companies: (1) They must obtain a special permit for landing from the Ministry of Communications of the National Government and pay a fixed rent. (2) The company is only allowed to relay overseas telegrams. (3) They are not allowed to directly receive and send telegrams. (4) The company should maintain the submarine cables in perfect condition, and if there is any damage or obstruction, they must be repaired promptly. (5) Increase the telegraph fees due to China. (6) In the event of major domestic or international incidents, the National Government reserves the right to send personnel to inspect and supervise, and temporarily take over the operation. (7) The above special permission is limited to a period of two years. It has been investigated that Zhuang Zhihuan's summary of the negotiations regarding telecommunications submarine cables stated that the most important six points were agreed upon, including (1) the validity period of the landing permit is from five to ten years, etc. It has been investigated that the landing of submarine cables is not explicitly stipulated in the contract but is only marked in official documents. Now, Zhuang Zhihuan has proposed this condition, which is to provide a layer of protection for the landing patent right that has never been stipulated in the contract. Not only has the landing patent right not been cancelled in the contract, but the protection of the landing patent right has been increased in the contract. This violates the Ministry of Communications' claim that no government, company, or individual of any country will be granted exclusive rights to land submarine cables in the future, and it also fails to comply with the Ministry of Communications' proposed method of canceling all patent privileges. Nothing could be worse than this surrender of national rights. Even if concessions are made in negotiations, they should comply with Clause 7 of Item E of the Ministry of Communications, which limits the special permission period to two years. On what basis did Zhuang Zhihuan make concessions to five to ten years? Once the company has obtained a license, then within five or ten years, all landing patent rights will not only not be cancelled in fact, but also be protected by law. If this agreement is finalized, then within these five or ten years, our country will lose its sovereignty over communications, which will be no different from before. Furthermore, it has been investigated that the Ministry of Communications proposed a solution: (C) The Ministry of Communications should notify the two companies to immediately recover all borrowed lines, and take over all agency submarine cables by the end of this year (i.e., the end of the 19th year). Now, Zhuang Zhihuan first stated that the connection from the submarine cable landing point to the Shanghai company's operations room should be borrowed by the Department of Electrical Affairs of the Ministry of Communications for the company's use, and the Department of Electrical Affairs should be responsible for repairs and maintenance. Then, he stated that only the necessary lines should be connected to the company's operations and submarine cables, and the rest should be managed and used by our country's telegraph bureau. The Ministry of Communications proposed a solution, advocating that all borrowed lines should be recovered and taken over independently, but Zhuang Zhihuan actually allowed the company to borrow them, which clearly contradicts the Ministry of Communications' method of recovering all borrowed lines and agency submarine cables. Moreover, the standard for what constitutes a 'necessary line' has not been clearly specified, which will undoubtedly be determined by the company. If it is determined by the company, then which line is not a necessary line, i.e., which line is not a borrowed line, and the Ministry of Communications' so-called recovery and Zhuang Zhihuan's so-called 'the rest shall be managed and used by our country's telegraph bureau' will all become empty words. Any line borrowed by the company is a line that our country cannot directly manage. If this is the case, then the autonomy of international communications will be completely lost again. Furthermore, it has been investigated that the Ministry of Communications proposed a solution: (E) The former Qing government allowed the company to install submarine cables in our country's territorial waters without permission, and unconditionally allowed them to land and connect cables and operate freely. Such provisions that humiliated the country and harmed its rights should not be bound by the status of today's National Government. Therefore, in the minimum conditions, it is proposed that the company shall not be allowed to directly receive and send telegrams. If the company is not allowed to directly receive and send telegrams, then the right to receive and deliver telegrams should be taken back by the Ministry of Communications and exercised freely. Now, Zhuang Zhihuan first advocated that the matters of delivery and reception should be entrusted to the company by the Chinese government and supervised by personnel, and a sign of the Chinese Telegraph Bureau could be hung outside the building. Then, he advocated that the reception and dispatch matters should be handled entirely by our country's telegraph bureau, and the company's current employees could be entrusted to gain proficiency. The so-called hanging of the Chinese Telegraph Bureau's sign outside the building indicates that the internal organization will remain unchanged. The so-called company's current employees can be entrusted, which indicates that our country's personnel and administrative power will be restricted. This kind of perfunctory approach will not only make neighboring countries laugh but also embarrass our people. Foreigners enjoy the benefits of free business operations, while our country enjoys the empty name of receiving and sending telegrams. What is the purpose of making such concessions? In summary, the issue of apportioning telegraph fees has not been reported, and the losses involved, based only on what is known from hearsay, are that compared to the old contract, the reporting from the negotiating authorities believes that the annual increase in revenue is one million yuan, but in reality, there will still be losses of two to three million yuan or more. It has been investigated that in the old contract, the Chinese side received thirty-eight and a half centimes per word for apportioning telegraph fees. In the current draft contract, there are two types of fees: inland and Shanghai. The inland fee is sixty centimes, and the Shanghai fee is thirty-one centimes (a reduction of three and a half centimes compared to the old contract). According to the actual situation and business conditions, the Shanghai telegraph fees must be carefully calculated by experts in order to know the exact amount. Regarding the ratio between the inland and Shanghai fees, it is 80% to 20%. It is necessary to study the gains and losses in this regard. (The several points mentioned in the telegraph above are all important key points, and the other minor issues are too numerous to mention.) Now, on the day when the contract is being revised, it is the time when our country is recovering the autonomy of international communications that has been lost for fifty years. What is Zhuang Zhihuan doing? How dare he make one mistake after another, leading to the failure of the negotiations to this point? It can be seen that the accusations from the outside world are not without reason. Such dereliction of duty and surrender of rights should be impeached in accordance with Article 2 of the Impeachment Law. Is this appropriate? We request that it be submitted for review in accordance with the law."

Review Report Members: Gao Youtang, Shao Hongji, Zhou Lisheng

The review report on the impeachment case of Zhuang Zhihuan is as follows: "It is submitted for reporting. The President of the Yuan has assigned the impeachment case of Zhuang Zhihuan, Director of the Department of Electrical Affairs of the Ministry of Communications, for dereliction of duty and surrender of rights in handling international telecommunications and water and electricity negotiations, which was proposed by the three members Liu, Gao, and [unclear], to be reviewed by the three of us, Youtang, Hongji, and Lisheng. Youtang and others have carefully reviewed the original case and various related documents and unanimously believe that the allegations of dereliction of duty and surrender of rights against Zhuang Zhihuan in the original impeachment case are based on solid evidence and clear circumstances. Therefore, it should be submitted for disciplinary action in accordance with the law. Before the establishment of the disciplinary organs for officials, a rapid remedy of dismissal from office should be presented to the National Government in accordance with Article 7 of the Impeachment Law, and disciplinary action should be submitted after the establishment of the disciplinary organs for officials. All review opinions are compiled into a report in accordance with Article 7 of the Control Yuan Review Rules and submitted for review and implementation. It has been investigated that Zhuang Zhihuan has now been transferred to the position of Counselor by the Ministry of Communications. Although he has been removed from the position of Director of the Department of Electrical Affairs, he should still be removed from his current position and cannot avoid it due to the transfer. This is stated in combination."

Letter from the Bureau of Civil Affairs: The Bureau of Civil Affairs of the National Government sent a public letter to the Control Yuan, stating confidentially: "Having received Chairman's letter from Zhuang Zhihuan, presenting the handling of telecommunications submarine cable negotiations, being subject to unwarranted criticism, and respectfully submitting a summary of the negotiation process, earnestly requesting fairness and a thorough investigation of this case. According to the submitted summary and the negotiation outline of the Pacific Business Submarine Cable Company forwarded by the Executive Yuan, it is very different from the solution proposed by the Ministry of Communications in May of the 18th year and the secret submission of the negotiation process and future coping methods in October of the 19th year. Since Zhuang Zhihuan has requested a fair and thorough investigation, the entire case should be handed over to the Control Yuan for a thorough investigation and verification, and the Executive Yuan should be instructed to instruct the Ministry of Communications to be extra cautious about the progress of negotiations, to promptly seek remedies, and not to lose national rights in the slightest. The handling situation should be reported in detail at any time, etc. In addition to separate dispatches, the corresponding full volume is enclosed with a detailed list."

Zhuang Zhihuan's Letter: Zhuang Zhihuan's letter to Chairman Jiang Yun states: "Chairman, respectfully, it has been investigated that in November of last year, several people including Chen Yiyan accused Zhihuan of handling telecommunications submarine cable negotiations.

Current Affairs Commentary

The German Political Tide Suddenly Becomes Serious 32

Just when the German authorities are facing economic difficulties and urgently seeking compromise with neighboring countries in order to save themselves, the various political parties within the country believe that the authorities are disregarding the suffering of the people and that the emergency orders are too harsh. There is a sudden shift in the political situation. This further plunges the authorities into a dilemma. The German government, unable to remedy the financial shortage, has had no choice but to seek assistance from Britain on the one hand, hoping to revise the Young Plan to reduce its external burden, and on the other hand, to issue emergency orders to increase new taxes in order to balance government revenue and expenditure. This was originally the government's desperate attempt to save itself in a situation where it had no other choice. However, looking at its external hopes now, they are still in the realm of the unattainable. The political parties on the left and right within the country, as well as the various provincial groups, have risen up to unanimously resist the government's orders. According to a telegram from Berlin, after Brüning's return to Germany, there will be a major change internally. Demonstrations have already broken out in various places. This situation is sufficient to deal a major blow to the government's diplomatic efforts. Whether diplomacy is successful or not depends on the means of the diplomatic authorities, as well as on the stability of the domestic political situation. An unstable domestic political situation makes it easy for foreigners to observe and make excuses, which will stagnate diplomacy. Therefore, the German government today is in a position where it cannot but revise the emergency orders. On the party side, unless they are extreme advocates who want to overthrow the government and then be happy, they should not take excessive measures today, which would lead the country to an unmanageable predicament.

Important Foreign Telegrams

Recent Anglo-German Meeting Followed by Sudden Visit to Europe by U.S. Treasury Secretary 67

Leading to Speculation from All Sides

Germany Avoids Joining a European Group

To Confront American War Debts

Seeking to Rescue the Current Economic Crisis

Likely to Seek Help from the United States

German Emergency Decree

Draws Domestic Opposition

Reuter's, New York, 10th: U.S. Treasury Secretary Mellon departs for Europe today. Naturally, there is much speculation regarding the purpose of his trip. When asked, Mellon tersely replied that he does not wish to discuss war debts or reparations, and that his sole purpose is to visit his son at Oxford University.

Electric Communication, New York, 10th: U.S. Treasury Secretary Mellon's sudden departure for Europe today has caused quite a stir. It goes without saying that his trip is directly related to the recent Anglo-German meeting. It is possible that the originally anticipated meeting of U.S. Secretary of State Stimson and British Foreign Secretary Henderson with German leaders in Berlin may now materialize. Although Mr. Mellon stated before his departure that it was unrelated to war debts and reparations, sources from the government suggest that Mr. Mellon may directly discuss the matter with German representatives. With the Young Plan as its focus, the atmosphere in European and American political circles is becoming increasingly active.

National, Berlin, 10th: Chancellor Brüning and Foreign Minister Curtius returned to Berlin from England this afternoon. Accompanying them was U.S. Ambassador Sackett, who was invited to Germany by the Chancellor. When the Chancellor and his party departed from Bremerhaven to return to Berlin, a small group of National Socialists shouted slogans such as "Germany Wake Up! Death to Brüning!", leading to the arrest of several individuals. A similar incident occurred at the Friedrichstrasse station. Upon arriving in Berlin, the Chancellor convened a cabinet meeting that evening to report on the trip.

Associated Press, Berlin, 10th: The Associated Press has learned that Germany does not wish to join a European group to jointly confront the United States on the war debt issue. Instead, it will seek assistance from the United States to rescue its economic and financial crisis. Although the German government is urgently seeking the swift implementation of a three-year moratorium on reparations payments, it has no intention of implementing it before U.S. Secretary of State Stimson arrives in Germany. Mr. Stimson is currently scheduled to arrive in Berlin on July 21st for a one-week stay. British Foreign Secretary Henderson is also expected to arrive in Germany at the same time. At that time, the three countries' leaders will undoubtedly engage in discussions regarding the payment of war debts and reparations. It is expected that there will be subsequent consultations between Germany and France, and between Germany and Italy. When U.S. Treasury Secretary Mellon arrives in Europe, Germany is also expected to have diplomatic representatives contact him. Germany currently hopes that the meetings of important figures from various countries will result in an international reparations conference.

National, Rome, 10th: Italian public opinion has paid close attention to the Anglo-German Chequers meeting from the beginning. Now that the meeting has concluded, the newspapers place great emphasis on the increased friendship between England and Germany, and dismiss the pessimism of certain foreign newspapers as unfounded. As for the French Foreign Minister's statement that the Young Plan is inviolable, the Messaggero newspaper considers it insignificant, as Briand himself has repeatedly stated that he will continue his policy of reconciliation with Germany.

National, Berlin, 10th: After Chancellor Brüning's return to Germany, significant changes are expected in domestic politics. Although the parliament is currently in recess, the opposition parties on both the left and right have proposed convening parliament, which was dismissed today by the parliament's standing committee. However, since the issuance of the emergency decree, there has been obvious unrest within the country. The fact that it has not yet materialized is only to provide an opportunity for the various factions in parliament to consider it. Moreover, the measures adopted by the government are considered by the public to be too harsh. This is undeniable. In the future, when various factions rise up in opposition to the government, it is feared that the government will rely solely on the Centre Party. A political storm is brewing. Various labor unions, provincial organizations, war veterans, and so on have convened meetings in recent days and passed various protests, claiming that the suffering of the people has not only reached its limit but has also exceeded the possible range. All of this is forcing the various political parties to adopt a definite strategy. Therefore, parties such as the Democratic Party and the Economic Party have recognized in meetings that this emergency decree needs to be amended. Other parties, such as the Social Democratic Party, the largest party in Germany, and the Nationalist Party, have scheduled meetings for Friday to discuss this matter. The fate of the emergency decree hinges on this.

National, Berlin, 11th: Although the political world is currently focused on the outcome of the Anglo-German meeting, the domestic situation has suddenly become serious after Chancellor Brüning and his party returned to the country. Demonstrations against the recent emergency decree have taken place throughout the country. In many major cities such as Frankfurt and Hamburg, unemployed workers have rioted due to hunger, marching in crowds and seizing bread and food along the way. When the police intervened, bloody conflicts often resulted. The government has been forced to abandon everything else and focus on resolving this matter. The Chancellor has invited the leaders of the major political parties to meet this afternoon and evening, hoping to reach a compromise on the emergency decree, make slight changes to it, and avoid further political turmoil so that cabinet members can focus on planning financial and economic relief programs.

New Invention: Tubercle Bacillus Delipidification Technique 68

(1) (Translated from the latest German Journal of Tuberculosis)

Since Dr. Koch discovered the tubercle bacillus as the pathogen of pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., consumption), tuberculosis scholars in the East and West have striven to study it, hoping to find a wonderful way to kill this bacillus. However, the results have all ended in failure. This is because general physicians in the past did not understand the special structure of tubercle bacilli, thinking that all bacteria could be killed with disinfectant medicines, either by internal administration or injection, just like injecting "606" for syphilis. It was only after Dr. Bergell's painstaking research that he published that tubercle bacilli have a special defense force that can resist attacks from all external medicinal forces. This is because tubercle bacilli are composed of a neutral fat inner membrane and an acid-fast wax outer membrane (Llipoid). Unless a way is found to destroy its wax defense line and disarm its fatty armament, there is no way to capture tubercle bacilli and put them to death. Moreover, when tubercle bacilli invade a local part of the human body, their surroundings are eroded to form stubborn nodules that obstruct the passage of blood flow, causing the general disinfectant medicines injected or taken internally to be unable to cross the threshold. Just like a specially martial-lawed restricted area, medicinal power cannot reach the affected area. Therefore, even if the whole body is immersed in a medicine pool, it cannot harm the hair of the tubercle bacilli. Therefore, the only combat strategy to eliminate tubercle bacilli must at least have the following two decisive conditions:

(1) The medicinal power must be able to destroy the nodules and reach the affected area directly.

(2) It must also be able to strip or dissolve the waxy and fatty inner and outer membranes.

Only in this way can it achieve the success of breaking through barriers and slaying generals. Otherwise, it is like scratching an itch through boots. Under these two guarantees, the tubercle bacilli secretly laugh at people's inability to harm them.

(2)

Hammershaly and Terebensky discovered that the acid-fastness of tubercle bacilli is due to the ability of wax to resist acid. Therefore, they applied 5% to 10% caustic potash solution to remove the acid-fast wax of tubercle bacilli. Later, Moussn and Goupjl applied chlorine gas to remove the acid-fast wax. However, this delipidification method can only be applied to staining methods for microscopic examination, because its medicinal properties are highly toxic and ultimately cannot be practically applied to the human body.

In recent years, there have been occasional cases where chaulmoogra oil has been applied to leprosy and achieved unexpected results. This is because leprosy bacilli and tubercle bacilli are acid-fast bacteria of the same nature, and chaulmoogra oil has the effect of delipidification and has a bactericidal power more than a hundred times that of carbolic acid. As a result, general scholars have aroused enthusiastic attention and thought of applying chaulmoogra oil to patients with tuberculosis in hopes of achieving results. They used various chemical methods to extract the main components of chaulmoogra oil. However, it is only limited to skin and superficial tuberculosis and can achieve good results. For deep organ tuberculosis, such as the lungs, liver, and kidneys, it still cannot achieve any effect.

(3)

Therefore, Dr. Bergell, the great teacher of tuberculosis patients all over the world, went a step further, collecting various medicinal substances of animal, plant, and mineral origin and painstakingly researching them, hoping to obtain a delipidifying effect without the various shortcomings of chaulmoogra oil. He worked tirelessly for decades, wondering how much brainpower and effort he had exhausted to seek the most rational and purest chemical agent. Finally, he discovered that in the compressed juice of the mesenteric glands of special animals, there is a certain effective ingredient that has a strong delipidifying effect on tubercle bacilli. He immediately applied this new ingredient to tubercle bacilli and performed the Ziehl-Neelsen staining method. It no longer stained red but stained blue. This result is completely the same as other non-acid-fast bacteria. Since then, the claim that it is impossible to artificially remove the acid-fastness of tubercle bacilli, which was regarded by physicians in the East and West, has been completely overturned. He seized the highest authority in delipidifying bactericides and experimented with this compound on various types of tuberculosis in animals and humans, and all achieved great miraculous effects without side effects. This is really a new dawn in the treatment of pulmonary tuberculosis, a major question in the medical community for thousands of years.

(4)

After the etiology and pathology of pulmonary tuberculosis were clarified, Dr. Bergell's great medical saint's invented new medical theory on the ideal treatment of pulmonary tuberculosis was also experimented and achieved great success. "Sanosin," the only and unparalleled special medicine for pulmonary tuberculosis in the 20th century, was produced in accordance with this new medical theory and new doctrine, opening up a new record in the medical community. The main components contained in "Sanosin" are listed below.

The chemical name of the first ingredient is Aminoaethylsulfonsaeure (C2h7nso3), which is extracted from the mesenteric gland liver of special animals and the blood of marine mollusks. Its chemical properties are colorless and transparent, and it is a shiny tetrad or hexad crystal. At 12 degrees Celsius, it can dissolve in 16 times of cold water, and it is easier to dissolve in hot water, but it cannot dissolve in anhydrous alcohol and ether. If it is boiled with a strong saline solution, it becomes acetic acid and sulfuric acid. When fused with mercury, it forms a white powder that is insoluble in water. If it is decomposed at 240 degrees Celsius and mixed more closely with several parts of soda ash, it is heated on a platinum plate to produce a residue. According to the experimental report of Dr. Sohroder, this ingredient can directly act on tubercle bacilli and dissolve the wax and fat of its outer membrane. Once the tubercle bacillus loses this strategic barrier, it cannot avoid its death penalty. Moreover, this ingredient also has a considerable stimulating effect, which can increase the secretion of bile in patients, and the function of metabolism becomes more vigorous. For lung diseases, it can also change its connective tissue and achieve a therapeutic effect.

The second ingredient is KalllumSulfoouaiecolloum (C6Ｈ5ＯＨ)(OCH)2So2OK, created by Dr. Tiemsnn, which can enhance the resistance of tuberculosis patients and the coagulation power of serum, promote metabolism, increase white blood cells, prevent the development of tubercle bacilli, and has the special functions of strengthening the stomach, eliminating phlegm, and disinfecting. Therefore, since Dr. Reichenbach, a famous modern tuberculosis physician, advocated its application in pulmonary tuberculosis, physicians in Germany and the United Kingdom have regarded this ingredient as the supreme sacred product for the treatment of tuberculosis.

(5)

"Sanosin," a new medicine, is made by combining the above two major valuable main ingredients. Therefore, "Sanosin" is an unprecedented special new medicine for the treatment of pulmonary tuberculosis, which indeed has great value. The therapeutic effects are listed below.

(1) When the medicinal power of "Sanosin" is tested in a test tube, tubercle bacilli all lose their acid-fastness after one minute, and after three minutes, the pulmonary tuberculosis bacilli are completely killed without exception.

(2) When "Sanosin" is applied to the human body by internal administration or injection, it can penetrate into the interior of various organs such as the lungs. After 18 hours, examination of the urine can reveal the reaction of DIBZO. After 48 hours, this reaction disappears, and white blood cells increase significantly.

(3) According to animal experiments, "Sanosin" can penetrate into the tuberculosis lesions. When examining the latent tubercle bacilli in the lesions, they all lose their acid-fastness. This proves that its wax is completely dissolved.

(4) After taking "Sanosin" internally for about a week, you can see the dilution of sputum, the decrease in body heat, and the pleasant state of mind and body. (5) If you continue to take "Sanosin" internally for more than one or two months, you can clearly see the weight gain, the appetite is stimulated, all symptoms are gradually alleviated, and finally, the great power of turning the tide is achieved.

Request by Chambers of Commerce in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province to Revise the Business Tax Law 72

And Request for Temporary Suspension of Promulgation and Implementation

The Business Tax Law has been drafted and passed by the Legislative Yuan. Chambers of Commerce in various counties of Jiangsu Province believe that the articles of the tax law greatly violate the General Outline for Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces decided by the Central Political Council, and the supplementary measures formulated by the Ministry of Finance. Furthermore, they failed to accommodate the repeated petitions from Chambers of Commerce in various counties of Jiangsu Province. Therefore, it was decided that the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce would again submit a joint petition to the Central Political Council, the National Government, and the Legislative Yuan, requesting that the passed Business Tax Law be revised separately based on the principles decided upon. The original telegram is recorded below: "As reported, the Business Tax Law passed by the Legislative Yuan, such as Article 4 of the original text, stipulates that the business tax rate should be 2/1000 to 10/1000 of the total business revenue as the standard, and 4/1000 to 10/1000 of the business capital as the standard, which exceeds the range stipulated in Article 4 of the General Outline for Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces, that the business tax rate should be calculated using the per mille method according to the tax standard, and should not exceed 2/1000 at most, and some rates are as high as ten times that amount. Article 10 stipulates that the original Tooth Tax, Pawn Tax, Slaughter Tax, and other business taxes in various provinces and cities that should be banned or levied by means of prohibition according to law may be temporarily changed to business tax according to the original tax rate, which also contradicts Article 7 of the General Outline for Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces, which stipulates that after the implementation of the business tax, all the original tooth certificate tax, pawn certificate tax, slaughter tax, etc. in various provinces, as well as other taxes and levies with the same nature as the business tax, should be abolished, and Article 11 of the supplementary measures formulated by the Ministry of Finance, that although tooth tax, pawn tax, slaughter tax, and other taxes and levies with the same nature as the business tax must be merged separately in accordance with the outline, in order to temporarily take care of local revenue, it can be handled in two steps. The first step is to change the name of tooth, pawn, slaughter, and other taxes to business tax, and the tax rate is still levied according to the original tax rate of tooth, pawn, and slaughter taxes as a temporary transitional measure. The second step is to change the above-mentioned original tax rate to business tax rate after the business tax is handled properly, so as to unify the regulations, which are also inconsistent. This clearly violates the meaning of the General Outline for Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces decided by the 270th Central Political Council and the principles of the supplementary measures formulated by the Ministry of Finance, and the legislation contains fixedness, and the use of the words 'temporary' is also not seen in legal texts, which seems inappropriate. This should be specifically corrected. In accordance with the principles decided by the Central Political Council, it seems that the important regulations of the General Outline for Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces and the supplementary measures formulated by the Ministry of Finance, such as Article 6 of the supplementary measures formulated by the Ministry of Finance, that for businesses that sell goods, and the amount of business income is used as the tax standard, the tax rate for wholesale business can be appropriately reduced compared to retail business, and Article 12 that the field tax in various provinces originally has the distinction between provincial tax and county tax, and since the business tax comes from the county people, its burden nature is the same as the field tax. In the future, how much of the business tax collected should be allocated and retained for county use, and the provincial government should consider the loss of the county and properly allocate it, and the money allocated should be used first for the undertakings that have insufficient funds due to the reduction of the tax, so that they can be continued, etc., should be adopted as much as possible when formulating the Business Tax Law and clearly stipulated, so as to reflect the spirit of the Central Government's decision that day. This should be ordered to be supplemented. In addition, Article 4 of the Business Tax Law passed by the Legislative Yuan stipulates that the business tax rate, with the amount of net business income as the standard, the tax rate is changed to a percentage, at least 2% and up to 10%, which is beyond the scope of the General Outline for Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces and the supplementary measures formulated by the Ministry of Finance approved by the Central Political Council. Its nature is similar to income tax. I don't know which businesses can apply the net income tax assessment, and there is no clear provision, which is easy to cause disputes. This should be ordered to be clearly stipulated. Furthermore, the main point of the repeated petitions of the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce is that the business tax, in terms of its nature, is a behavior tax, and should only be taxed equally based on whether the behavior exists or not. After our country's tax reduction, the central government has mostly separately changed to unified tax for various important commodities, and the unified tax rate mostly uses a percentage, which is higher than the previous tax. If the provinces levy business tax on their behavior again, it seems to be a double tax, and the tax rate itself cannot

Page 9

Brief News Summary 73

Try hard to reduce it. Therefore, in the 17th year of the Republic of China, the central government convened a meeting to reduce taxes and decided that the business tax rate should be calculated using the per mille method according to the tax standard, and should not exceed 2/1000 at most. If it is called per mille, but the tax rate is above 10/1000, it is avoiding the name of percentage and using the reality of percentage, which is absolutely unbearable for merchants. The commerce of Jiangsu Province is closely related to that of Shanghai. If the measures for the business tax in Jiangsu Province are slightly different from those in Shanghai, it will inevitably affect the prosperity of inland commerce and put merchants in a more deadly situation. There are a total of two points, detailed in the original petition, which should be taken into consideration. The important principles of the business tax in Shanghai, as reported, are five items: 1. The tax rate should not exceed 3/1000 at most, calculated by rounding. 2. Tax collection does not distinguish between Chinese and foreign merchants, and the tax amount does not distinguish between domestic and foreign goods. 3. Wholesale businesses are levied at 1/4 of the rate. Manufacturers who directly retail their manufactured goods still pay tax according to the tax rate stipulated for manufacturing, and are not subject to additional business tax for sales. 4. Brokers who accept entrustment to act as agents are exempt from business tax. 5. If the business operator reports the amount of business, and it is certified by an accountant or chamber of commerce, the investigation procedure can be exempted. The business tax law passed by the Legislative Yuan has higher tax rates than those in Shanghai, and it may be difficult to force Shanghai to cut its feet to fit the shoes. The measures for everything, regarding the decision of the Central Political Council, should pay attention to not disturbing the people and not hindering commercial development, and it is not as thorough as Shanghai, which will inevitably hinder the development of inland commerce and make it impossible for merchants to operate. This should be rescued. It concerns the creation of a new tax and violates the decision-making principles. Our association and other representatives of merchants, are concerned about the current interests and the life and death in the future, it is really difficult to remain silent. I am using another telegram to state, I beg you to examine the Legislative Yuan to revise separately based on the decision-making principles and temporarily delay the implementation in order to protect the commercial business and avoid the hindrance, I am very grateful to be waiting for your order."

Songjiang 74

Organizational Problems in the Administrative Conference. The third county administrative conference of this session suddenly had a problem of illegal organization yesterday (11th), which was the second day of the conference. According to the provisions of Article 2, Section 2 of the Organizational Regulations of the Administrative Conference, the number of appointed members shall not exceed half of the number of ex officio members. Currently, there are 26 ex officio members and 15 appointed members, which exceeds the statutory number. It is feared that the implementation of the bills in the future will be hindered. Therefore, the district chiefs jointly submitted a report to County Magistrate Jin for correction. I don't know how this case will be resolved.

Kunshan 75

Suicide of a Traveler in the Datong Hotel. A person from Shaxi went to the Datong Hotel at Zhengyang Bridge on the 9th and claimed to be Qian Zhonghe, 24 years old, a primary school teacher. The porter led him to Room 6 to rest. At 10 pm, he closed the door and went to sleep. Qian felt that the environment was bad and suddenly had the thought of leaving the world. He committed suicide by taking poison. Until 1 pm on the 10th, the porter went to knock on the door. After calling for a long time, there was no response. Knowing that there was a change, he managed to pry open the door and saw Qian lying stiffly in bed with a pale face. Knowing that he had taken poison, he immediately reported to the accounting room and reported to the Public Security Bureau. Qian was sent to Guangren Hospital for treatment. According to the doctor, he had taken anesthetic powder. Fortunately, the amount taken was small, and his life could be saved. However, it was still difficult to wake up for a while, so he remained in the hospital. Qian's relative, Mr. Wu, urgently sent a letter to his family to come to Kunshan.

Unlawful Police Officer Sent to the County Government for Punishment. Luo Qixiang, the captain of the Kunshan County Police Team, usually restrained his subordinates, which was quite strict. However, the police officers often had conflicts with people when they went out. On the 10th, a police officer Cai, dressed in plain clothes, boarded a ship to Qian Dun without a ticket. The ticket seller, unaware that Cai was a police officer, ordered him to buy a ticket in accordance with the regulations. Cai not only refused to buy a ticket, but also beat the ticket seller severely. The passengers on the same ship were in an uproar. Wang Liang, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, stepped forward to dissuade him, and was insulted and scolded by Cai. Wang saw that there was no reasoning, and called the police officer to accompany the police officer to the Public Security Bureau Substation on the road to explain the ins and outs to Inspector Lu Zhongying. The police officer beat Director Wang again. Inspector Lu believed that the police officer was unreasonable and sent the police officer to the County Police Team Department. After Captain Luo inquired about the previous situation, he believed that the police officer had no regard for the law and immediately dismissed him. He was sent to the Public Security Bureau again. After Director Qin briefly interrogated him, he submitted a document to the county government on the 11th for legal action.

The county government strictly ordered the arrest of the bandits and captured the chief bandit Tan Laoer, also known as Dai A'er, also known as Cai Jixian. He confessed to colluding to kidnap, extort, and kill without denying it. The county government detailed the report to the provincial government for approval of execution. On the morning of the 10th, the county government sent a reviewing officer Yang to take the seat in the lobby, signed and brought the criminal to the execution ground for execution.

Wuxi 77

Horrifying News of Strangling Children to Death in the Middle of the Night. Sun Haoming, a resident of Shituwan East Street, District 16 (Wan'an City), used to open Wanfeng Jinghuo Store in the town. Later, due to poor business, he had to close down. Sun is now 47 years old and has three sons and one daughter, and is addicted to opium pills. The eldest son, Ye Sun, 26 years old, is also addicted to opium pills. He married the daughter of Zhang Zixian of Xizhang. He has one son and one daughter. He used to work in the fruit shop opened by his father-in-law in Suzhou. Because his father-in-law smoked opium pills, he was very lazy in his work, so he resigned the year before last. After Ye Sun returned home, he still did not repent and still associated with opium pills. His father, Haoming, hated him for this, so he often beat Ye Sun. The night before yesterday, he locked him in the bathroom with iron chains, and then strangled him to death with hemp rope with his daughter, Yue Xian. The next day, he told people that his son had committed suicide. The wife and mother of the deceased learned that Ye Sun's death was unclear, and planned to have serious negotiations with Haoming in the next few days.

Reassignment of the Second District Chief of the Water Police. Mao Mujun, the chief of the Second District of the Provincial Public Security Team stationed in Wuxi, has been in office for two years. Recently, Hu Pu'an, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, ordered him to be transferred to the province for appointment. The vacant position was concurrently held by Shen Gaojin, the current chief of the Third District. The handover must be completed within days.

County Government Convenes a Meeting on Business Tax. The Wuxi Rice Industry Association recently saw in the newspaper that the Zhejiang rice industry has been approved by the Zhejiang Provincial Government to exempt rice from business tax, as rice is an essential item for people's livelihood. The cases of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are the same, and Wujin and other counties have already telegraphed to the ministries and provinces, requesting exemption. Therefore, they are still adopting a wait-and-see attitude on the recognition and payment of business tax. The Wuxi Business Tax Bureau believes that the opening of business tax is imminent, and the amount recognized and paid by various industries has a rough idea. It is difficult for the rice industry to be unique. It specially discussed with County Magistrate Pan and the Provincial Committee, and Director Yang of the Business Tax Bureau, and invited Zhao Zixin and other leaders of the eight sections of the rice industry, and all standing members of the County Chamber of Commerce, to hold a meeting at the County Government yesterday (11th) afternoon to discuss and solve the problem as soon as possible. There was also a discussion on the issue of provincial orders for borrowing.

The county government received a telegram from the provincial government, ordering the recruitment of 70 laborers to be sent to the province in three phases on the 16th, 20th, and 22nd. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Peng ordered the 14 district chiefs to recruit five people from each district and send them to the county on the 14th, 19th, and 24th, and they must handle the matter carefully and must not extort under the pretext.

Silk Cocoon Shops in Urban and Rural Areas Suspend Weighing One After Another. A total of more than 30 silk cocoon shops in the city and countryside have reported their opening this year. They have been open for seven days. Because there are very few goods arriving, they have all lowered prices to receive goods. The highest price has reached 80 yuan, but there are still few goods, only 2.50% of the harvest. Most of the shops have decided to suspend weighing on the 10th. The Cocoon Office, due to the order of the county magistrate, collects cocoon donations according to the plan to supplement local public security and other expenses, 35 cents per load. The cocoon merchants generally do not recognize this because the cocoon market is declining. A meeting will still be held on the 10th to resolve the issue.

Jiang Yunlong had already fled after hearing the news. When the order was issued, the inspectors were ordered to comply and go to the county government to handle it diligently. However, after a long time, the amount of bonds reported and released by the counties was still very small. The Construction Bond Fund Management Committee sent a letter requesting the department to select competent personnel to bring construction bond tickets and go to various counties to help promote sales. In fact, there are many difficulties. It is only necessary to inform the counties to entrust the sale of a certain amount, and immediately report the mail for approval by the hall. The bonds will be issued immediately and forwarded to the purchaser for collection in order to strengthen the public's trust. Therefore, it has instructed the county magistrates to comply with the previous orders and to promote the sale of construction bonds as soon as possible and raise the full amount in the shortest possible time.

Liyang Embezzlement Case Transferred to the Court. The provincial government, after receiving the telegrams from both parties, believed that the case should be thoroughly investigated and handled no matter what. In addition to the resolution to suspend both Li and Pan from their posts, it was also decided to transfer the case to the Zhenjiang District Court for trial in accordance with the law.

Although the police局 has conducted thorough investigations, it is still difficult to solve the cases. A few days ago, Zhang Hongquan, a cattle dealer, recently bought six heads from Nanshan in preparation for sale. Unexpectedly, in the thunderstorm last night, they were suddenly stolen. By the time they were discovered, it was too late to chase them. Fortunately, the two cattle lost by Wang Gouxang's family in the seventh vice-district yesterday were intercepted by neighbors halfway and were able to be saved. Others such as Zhang Tang Wang Xingmei, Wattana Lu Caizhong, Salt Industry You Quansheng and other families, have also been visited by thieves one after another, suffering huge losses. It is said that there are many fellow parties in the group, and the method of stealing is extremely clever. The place where they steal is mostly the junction of the two counties and the seawall, so it is easy to escape, so the arrest is particularly difficult. Li Zhibin, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, has taken this into consideration. In addition to patrolling the main ports of water and land, and checking, he also sent letters to neighboring counties yesterday to investigate together.

All are limited to be compiled and reported before June 17.

When he passed the Toutoubao on the Yellow River beach, he saw three bandits in long gowns and one bandit in short clothes holding short guns. They took Ding's luggage. The woman was from Shimatou, so many people on the line did not dare to walk.

Wei Yousan's Troops Harass Su and Si. Wei Yousan's bandits in Suqian Siyang have been harassing Su and Si for years, and the people cannot bear it. Now, the bandit leader Wei Yousan was pursued by the troops stationed in northern Anhui in a hurry and fled back to Jiangsu Province, searching for Baowei and other places, and joined forces with the bandit Liu Ershuizi and others, with about 500 people, wantonly harassing. As a result, the villagers at the junction of Su and Si counties dare not harvest wheat and are difficult to block. Liang Guanying, the general commander of the 20th Shilu Army, heard the news and thought that since the green gauze tent period was approaching and the villagers were busy with farming, if they were not severely suppressed, it would be difficult to deal with the deep roots. He telegraphed Liu Guoming, the brigade commander of the 95th Brigade, to dispatch troops to encircle and suppress them nearby.

Li Baokui and Hu Baomei, bandits from Yongjia County, were arrested along with the bandit leader Zheng Jizuo on the 9th. They kidnapped Chen Weiyan's child Jin Zhencan and extorted a ransom. Free Talk – World Anecdotes – Hai Ke

The artificial eyes made by Europeans have recently become more perfect. Not only can they be mistaken for real ones at a glance, but even the pupils can enlarge and contract, just like real eyes.

The most famous musician in the British royal family is Prince George. He plays the piano well and is known as a piano expert.

A French government expert on deafness says that wives must speak softly and respectfully to their husbands. If they nag their husbands day and night in a sharp voice, the husband can raise it as a reason for divorce if he cannot bear it.

The Hampton Court in England recently held a dog show, where dogs competed in begging, shaking hands, barking, and other activities. Those with excellent results received prizes.

The world record for altitude in aviation for men belongs to Lieutenant Soucek of the US Navy, with a height of 43,166 feet. The women's record belongs to an American woman, Miss E. Smith, with a height of 32,500 feet.

Paris, the capital of France, has a population of 4 million. The annual food consumption is estimated at 2 billion tons. The wine consumption is estimated at 6,775,800 gallons. The average meat consumption is 90 tons per person.

Brief Notes on the Game of Weiqi – Chen Boying

During the Daoguang period of the Qing Dynasty, there was a Beijing official named Li Fuhou, who loved playing Weiqi. He hired a national master, surnamed Bao, as his teacher. A colleague named Xie Yiqun also had a strong interest in the game, and they became friends. They met every day and played Weiqi whenever they met. Xie's skills were superior to Li's, and Li often found himself in difficult situations. One day, Li lost again, and Xie became arrogant and spoke sarcastically. Li was angry, and Xie left. Li rearranged the pieces, trying to find a way to survive, but he couldn't. It was midnight, and he still hadn't gone to the inner chamber. A maid named A Juan was serving him. She said, "It's late. Why hasn't the master gone to bed yet? Madam is sitting by the lamp, waiting for the sound of your footsteps. Every moment feels like a year. How can you bear it?" Li angrily scolded her. A Juan said, "Does the master want to avenge the humiliation of the day? It's easy. Just move one piece on the fourth or sixth row three steps to the left, and you'll turn defeat into victory." Li followed her advice, and it worked. He was delighted and asked her to play a game with him. A Juan won decisively. Li said, "I didn't expect you to have such skills. Can you compete with Xie?" A Juan said, "I see Xie as taking something from a bag. Skill is not a concern." Li asked her who she learned from. A Juan said, "I never learned. Last year, I watched the master play with guests and guessed the outcomes correctly. This year, I notice flaws in every game." Li was even happier and embraced her, saying, "Fortunately, there's a female Zhuge Liang to help your father vent his anger." The next day, Xie came. Li said to him, "There's a little girl who can distinguish black and white and discuss tactics. Please teach her generously." Xie agreed. A Juan came out and took the white pieces, saying to Xie, "Let the master make the first move." Xie was displeased. After ten moves, he realized her moves were extraordinary and responded seriously. After dozens of moves, he was at a disadvantage and racked his brains, holding a piece for a long time without knowing where to place it. A Juan said to Xie, "Why are you so lost in thought? My feet are weak, and I can't stand for long." In the middle of the game, Xie's position became more precarious, and sweat poured down his face. A Juan said, "It's not hot today. Why are you sweating so much? Are you sick? Should you take medicine?" The game ended with Xie only having a small corner, about the size of a palm, with only a few dozen pieces alive. He was greatly ashamed and fled. A Juan then said to Li, "How was it? Playing with Xie doesn't require any thought. It's boring. But even the national master Bao is not to be feared." Another day, the national master came, and A Juan played a game with him, again taking the white pieces. The national master was surprised and didn't dare to be careless. After thirty moves, the national master said, "I'm no match for you. I concede. I've lost five pieces in this game." He wanted to leave quickly, but Li insisted on finishing the game. After checking the pieces, it was confirmed. A Juan said to Bao, "You only lost one piece in this game. But in one place, you underestimated me and didn't block, so you lost more." The national master was convinced. Later, Li took A Juan as a concubine, and his skills improved daily. Few could compete with him.

Zhang Tianzhou of Wuxi said.

Record of the Flower Show in Suzhou – Wu Jiren

After the rambler rose blooms, the floral season wanes. The prosperity of Xipu lacks natural charm. A few days ago, I happened to return to Wu, and heard that there was a flower show in the Fifth of May Road Park. The organizer was my old friend, Mr. Fan Yunshu. Visiting flowers and old friends further stirred my interest. So, I went to see it with Fu Ji.

Entering the park gate, we first arrived at the East Study. Hundreds of potted flowers were on display. In the center, a small hill was piled up with colorful foreign flowers. The colors were coordinated and dazzling. Around the hall, potted flowers of various kinds were arranged. The jade-like blossoms and precious flowers swayed in the breeze. Flowers like the June Snow, Dendrobium loddigesii, and Chinese flowering crabapple, along with various azaleas, were splendid and radiant, displaying their beauty to the fullest extent. All were produced in this garden. The other varieties were too numerous to mention. Among them, we especially appreciated a type of fragrant narcissus, which we found particularly precious. There were four pots, all of the same color. The colors were like concubine river, goose yellow, water green, and moon white, possessing a charming beauty and emitting a rich, subtle fragrance that permeated the heart and soul. We lingered, reluctant to leave. Examining the labels, we found they belonged to the Yu family in Ge Baihu Lane, east of the city. Soon, we arrived at the West Pavilion. Dozens of species of Chinese juniper stumps were on display. At first glance, they looked like dead poplars sprouting buds, with a few twigs growing from rotten wood. Upon closer inspection, the intertwined roots and twisted trunks revealed a unique charm. Although shaped and pruned by human hands, they possessed an ancient and refined elegance, free from any trace of artificiality. The gnarled roots coiled like dragons, and the branches and leaves flourished, some towering like layered canopies, others soaring straight up like swirling snails, some like screens of cut rock, others like rounded spheres. The forms were novel and strange, full of vigor and vitality, lush and verdant, without any sign of decay or withering, conveying a sense of vigorous growth. I wondered how much effort the owner had put into cultivating them to achieve such a state. As far as my eyes could see, I offered some humble comments. I considered the pomegranate juniper of the Tianci Manor Li family to be the best, while the Podocarpus macrophyllus of the Qiaozhi Lane Zhang family, the Nandina domestica (Heavenly Bamboo) of the Yan Yamen Wang family (also known as Ten Merits), the Pinus thunbergii of the Ximei Lane Xu family, and the various small cacti were the highlights of the show. Afterwards, with plenty of leisure, I recorded these thoughts with my pen.

Interesting Stories from the Cocoon Studio – Yan Cun

My friend Cheng Xiaoqing, a writer of detective novels, enjoys a great reputation at home and abroad. However, he has not been producing much lately, leading many avid readers to write and inquire. There are many letters every day, and even some from far away, asking Mr. Cheng to solve their mysteries. This shows the power of his works. Yesterday, I visited his residence and had a half-day conversation. Mr. Cheng shared some recent interesting events, including the fact that after the film adaptation of his work "Shadow on the Window" by the Mingxing Film Company, he suddenly received a job offer from Guangdong. This was one incident. Another was that a reader from Shanghai asked if the investigations in "Shadow on the Window" were actually conducted by Xiaoqing himself. I then asked Xiaoqing about the structure of "Shadow on the Window." Xiaoqing said, "It's just a little trick. One night, I was returning home and saw a shadow in a building from afar. This made me think of my novels, and I wrote it down. It's very convoluted, but the source of the material can be triggered by a single event." I then asked Xiaoqing about his thoughts on detective films. Xiaoqing said, "The best ones use a convoluted plot as the warp and the detective steps as the weft. The next best only narrate the detective's abilities, neglecting the other characters in the drama. The worst ones only focus on fighting. Films like Ms. Bao Lian's long detective stories are really inferior. I recently watched 'The Rebirth of Sherlock Holmes,' which didn't fully capture the strengths of Holmes in the novel. I believe that detective films should not neglect the plot. They must be like peeling a banana or unraveling a cocoon to reveal the craftsmanship. Otherwise, they will be rough, confusing, and tasteless." I agree with Xiaoqing's words and believe that "Shadow on the Window" will set a new record for detective films. As evidenced by the facts, foreign detective films like "Everything Comes to Light" are rough compared to "Shadow on the Window."

The "After the Rain, Clear Sky" Premiere – Ni Gulian

At midnight on June 3rd, the Huaguang Sound Film Company, at the invitation of Mr. Luo Mingyou of the Lianhua Company, held a private premiere of its new sound film, "After the Rain, Clear Sky," which was filmed in Japan, at the Shanghai Grand Theater. I happened to be there and enjoyed it thoroughly from beginning to end. Because this film has not yet been publicly released, I don't need to provide a detailed review. Simply put, "After the Rain, Clear Sky" is a success. Whether it's the direction, script, acting, dialogue, singing, background, cinematography, or sound recording (the calligraphy in the dozens of explanatory subtitles is quite eye-straining and not to be praised), it's pure art. As the first sound film produced by a Chinese company, it surpasses foreign sound films that emphasize singing over plot, bringing glory to China. Although some say that "After the Rain, Clear Sky" was filmed in Japan and cannot be considered entirely "Huaguang," I disagree. Art knows no borders. Cinema originated in the West. Ask the Chinese film industry, besides directing, acting, cinematography, and set design, what equipment, such as cameras, film projectors, sound recorders, etc., is not foreign-made? Purchasing sound film equipment requires millions of capital. Who would dare to try it lightly? Now, Huaguang Company has used its wisdom and agility to first film a Movietone film in Japan, and it has succeeded. In the future, they will certainly officially purchase equipment and film domestically. Other companies will definitely follow suit and strive to produce truly domestic sound films. I pray that our entire Chinese film industry will regain its light and have a bright future. I have specifically written down my thoughts after watching "After the Rain, Clear Sky" to report to those who cherish Chinese cinema. Please everyone, rise up and support this promising Chinese cinema.

Travels around the Yellow Sea (28) – Huang Yanpei

"The fourth type of person strives for progress from their own position." This is what I have been telling young people for the past twenty years. Not working hard is not an option. Working hard without the right method is also not an option. Only by working hard can you find the right method. Everyone has their own position. When studying, studying is your foundation. Once you identify a field of study and master it to a certain degree, you should use what you have learned and serve. Whether it's directly for the country or indirectly for the country by serving society, within the scope of your responsibility, you should use a solid and persistent approach. First, seek internal refinement. Once you have sufficient strength, then seek external development while still adhering to the principle of using what you have learned. This is the most honorable, stable, and effective path for an individual to establish themselves. It is also the only way for the nation to save itself and become strong. The president of a Japanese university has held the position for over twenty or thirty years. A scholar at the Bikai Chicken Hatchery lectured us on how to construct chicken coops, how to mix feed, and how to incubate and raise chickens. He spoke for over an hour, tirelessly. Others may think the issue is too small. But his mindset seems to be that no cause is greater or more interesting than raising chickens. Thinking back, this is the true embodiment of their national spirit. Can Edison's contributions to the war effort in his laboratory be said to be smaller than that of soldiers in the trenches? Thinking this way, it is ridiculous to just wave flags and shout "Save the country!" or "Boycott foreign goods!" What China needs now is for millions of farmers, workers, businessmen, scholars, and soldiers to work diligently in their respective positions. If something happens, everyone will unite and resist foreign aggression. If we can do this, what is there to fear?

Alright, enough said. China has a long history. The so-called "ancient sages and worthies, eminent scholars and elders" have already spoken a lot about this. In recent years, people have spoken even more thoroughly and extensively. Not only have they spoken about it, but they have also written it on paper, pasted it on walls, and posted it on electric poles. It can be said to be "dazzling and overwhelming." The question now is for everyone to quickly take action and do it. Quickly take action and do it.

Finally, I would like to introduce a very valuable statement. A Mr. Xia, who was on the same boat on the way back, said that the three things Chinese people should pay attention to in the future are: (1) unification; (2) production; and (3) national defense. We believe this is a very insightful statement.

At this time, Zhang Xiaosan'er was cursing the patrol officer. Gold Prices Suddenly Drop

The gold price turned slightly downward again yesterday, with fluctuations of up to eight taels from morning to night, resulting in a net decrease of seven taels. Sentiment was uneasy but there were no major changes. The silver market was slightly lower with more selling interest, and the European market was normal, so prices fell from the start. Later, although exchange rates narrowed by half a point, domestic prices eased instead. Various firms sold more than they bought, causing the market price to break through 810 taels, making the market feel even weaker. There were slight fluctuations of two or three taels, but sellers were still abundant, mostly due to a shortage of drafts. The silver market is expected to rise again, estimated at 807 taels in the afternoon.

However, private telegrams only indicated a decrease of one-eighth, so sentiment reversed. Tongtaichang, Qianchangxiang, Hongli and others all sold, dropping from 13.2 qian to 10 qian. House Confiscated for Harboring Bandits Returned After Appeal: The House is Property of Fu Kang Bank; Initial Confiscation Reasoning Not Sufficient

Cai Fulin, a comprador for the British American Tobacco Company, was kidnapped by bandits last winter. The police later apprehended the bandits and handed them over to the Special District Local Court, which found them guilty and sentenced them. The court also confiscated the house at 401 Wuding Road in the western part of Shanghai, as the landlord had rented it to the bandits for use as a base of operations. The house is owned by Fu Kang Bank and managed by Youcheng Real Estate Company. Since its confiscation, the bank has been unwilling to accept the decision and proposed a solution at a meeting of the Shanghai Real Estate Association. It was agreed that since the court's decision was deemed unfair, legal channels should be pursued to seek redress. Therefore, Fu Kang Bank hired lawyers Zhang Deqin and Shen Yuesheng to file an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The appeal detailed the house's rental history and the reasons why it should not have been confiscated, arguing that in August of last year, the manager reported that a man claiming to be Zhang Mingzhi had come to rent the house. As usual, they asked him to sign a lease and provide a guarantor. He found the Fu Chang mirror shop at 1196 Carter Road as guarantor and moved in. Less than two months later, at the end of September, he terminated the lease and moved out. The house and rent were handed over, and there were no disputes. The rent collector returned the rental guarantee to the guarantor, never anticipating such a significant incident and innocent involvement, even to the point of confiscation of the house. Article 5 of the regulations on punishing kidnappers stipulates that the house should only be confiscated based on the following facts: (1) The bandit organization was discovered in the house, (2) The guarantor cannot be identified. In this case, the bandits were not discovered in the house, and the guarantor was identified as the Fu Chang mirror shop. Therefore, it is a misapplication of the law and an unwarranted implication. If confiscation were deemed legal, then any hotel or place where bandits had once set foot would also be implicated and confiscated. The original sentence was inappropriate and should be revoked, and the house should be returned. Judge Song convened a hearing with the jury. Many owners were present in the courtroom. Lawyer Zhang presented the reasons for the appeal. The judge then questioned the owner of the Fu Chang mirror shop about the circumstances of guaranteeing the rental of the house at that time. Subsequently, the police lawyer and Lawyer Zhang debated the issue. Yesterday afternoon, the court delivered its verdict, stating: The original judgment regarding the confiscation of the house at 401 Wuding Road is revoked. The house at 401 Wuding Road, owned by Fu Kang Bank, shall be returned.

Disabled Soldier Defrauded of Money for Artificial Limb: Zhang Deting Convicted of Fraud and Sentenced to Ten Months in Prison

Zeng Youcheng, deputy battalion commander of the 3rd Battalion of the 162nd Brigade of the 54th Division of the Army, was wounded in his left arm while commanding operations in the war zone last year. The arm was subsequently amputated by a doctor, resulting in a disability. Not only could he not work, but his appearance was also unsightly. He was eager to get an artificial limb. In March of this year, he met Zhang Deting, a native of Shaoxing, in the capital. Since then, there was no news. Recently, Zeng came to Shanghai and questioned the Russian, showing him the receipts given by Zhang. After investigation by the Special District Local Court, Judge Feng sentenced Zhang Deting to ten months in prison and ordered him to repay Zeng Youcheng 400 yuan. Xu Chuchang was found not guilty. Zhang was not satisfied and hired lawyer Fan Gang to appeal. Judge Feng approved the appeal.

Carriage Owners Advised to Instruct Drivers to Strictly Adhere to Regulations

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Motor Vehicle Department issued a circular yesterday stating that privately owned carriages often fail to comply with traffic regulations, especially in busy downtown areas. They sometimes cut in front of other vehicles, drive two abreast, or ignore traffic lights and police signals. These violations could impede other vehicles and cause danger. The Council urges carriage owners to pay attention for their own safety and the convenience of the public. Carriage owners must strictly instruct drivers to comply with traffic regulations. If such incidents occur again, the Motor Vehicle Department has instructed the police to record the carriage number and issue a summons to the court, just as with automobiles. The Council hopes that carriage owners and passengers will remind drivers to avoid traffic violations. The Municipal Council also hopes to reduce the number of lawsuits.
