Zheng Ruigen Commits Suicide by Drowning

Zheng Ruigen, a 25-year-old employee of the Yuli Pharmacy in the Nanshi district, and a native of Cixi, Zhejiang, had worked at the pharmacy for a long time. On the 27th of the previous month, Zheng requested leave to return to Cixi. At around 4:30 PM that day, he took a car to the Taikoo Wharf and boarded the New Beijing steamship. Unexpectedly, after Zheng departed, many days passed without him arriving home or returning to work, causing suspicion. The pharmacy sent someone to inquire on the New Beijing ship and learned that Zheng had boarded the ship that day. That night, as the ship sailed out of Songkou, Zheng suddenly had suicidal thoughts for some reason, walked out of the cabin, and jumped off the deck into the sea while no one was watching. Passengers and staff on the ship discovered this, but it was already dark, making rescue impossible. The body quickly drifted away. Zheng was wearing a short shirt and a gold ring on his left finger, engraved with the words "De Li". The pharmacy notified his family and reported the incident to the Seventh District Public Security Bureau in Wusong, which forwarded it to the Wusongkou Lifesaving Bureau, requesting assistance in recovering the body.

Arsenal Test-Fires Cannons in Songhu Yesterday

The arsenal in Southern Shanghai dispatched soldiers to transport four 75mm field guns manufactured in 1905 to Songhu yesterday afternoon. They landed and fired more than ten rounds along the coastal dike in Baoshan, with excellent results. It is said that the Capital General Headquarters has ordered the guns to be transported to Beijing for use. Therefore, a further test was conducted. They returned to Shanghai at around 5 p.m.

Dispute Over the Hiring of Temporary Workers at the British American Tobacco Factory: Failure to Follow Factory Practices Leads to Unsuccessful Union Negotiations

The various sections of the British American Tobacco factory in Pudong have been adding workers and hiring temporary workers, which was previously handled by the section supervisors and foremen. Recently, the factory has been independently hiring temporary workers, causing dissatisfaction among the workers. They believe that the newly hired temporary workers are informants for the factory. The first representative meeting of the Pudong Cigarette Industry Union requested the factory to abolish this new method. The union sent representatives to negotiate with the factory, and the factory agreed to provide more permanent worker badges and stop hiring temporary workers. However, yesterday, seven temporary workers in the tin packaging section of the old factory were promoted to permanent workers. The workers in that section were dissatisfied and reported the matter to the union for negotiation. The union sent Liu Dehua, Xiao Changgeng, and Fei Keguang, along with a translator, to negotiate with the factory. During the negotiations, a Westerner named Lobs hit worker number 182, causing public outrage. Another Westerner named Siderworth brandished a pistol to threaten the workers. The workers were terrified, and the order was disrupted. The representatives of the section, fearing trouble, advised the workers to wait for a resolution. The workers left the factory peacefully, and the negotiations were suspended. The union immediately convened a meeting of all workers and decided to demand that the factory follow the labor-management mutual aid regulations and continue to follow factory practices when adding permanent workers. They also demanded that the factory severely punish the Westerner who threatened the workers with a gun. After the meeting, the union sent representatives Chen Peide, Gu Ruofeng, and Liu Dehua to the factory for a second round of negotiations. However, the factory refused to compromise. The union, fearing the expansion of the unrest, immediately submitted a report to the city's Party headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau for instructions. It is rumored that the male and female workers in that section will continue to strike today, awaiting mediation.

Sand Barge Explosion at Jin Ju Tai Causes One Death and Five Injuries: Crew Members' Families Involved in Lawsuit

The Jin Ju Tai sand barge, which travels between Shandong and Shanghai, transporting grain and other goods, loaded raw oil and other cargo last month and set sail from Shandong back to Shanghai. The day after setting sail, they encountered pirates. Several pirate ships sped towards them. Two other sand barges traveling with them fired cannons as a warning. The Jin Ju Tai sand barge also prepared to fire its cannon (all merchant ships have cannons in case of emergencies). During the process of loading gunpowder and ammunition, a member of the crew, Jin Wanyu (from Tongzhou), accidentally caused the cannon to explode. Jin was killed instantly, and crew members Lu San, Gu Asi, Sang Yuming, Li Er, and the captain (manager) of the ship, Zhang Defu, were injured to varying degrees. The ship sailed back to Shandong, where Jin's body was prepared for burial and temporarily placed in a funeral home, with plans to bring it back to Shanghai in the winter. The ship then notified the family of the deceased and sailed back to Shanghai, arriving yesterday. The deceased's maternal uncle, Sun Hengming, went to Zhang Defu's home (located in Gaoxiangtou, inside the Dadongmen) to inquire why the coffin had not been brought to Shanghai. Zhang replied that it was currently hot weather and they were concerned about the spread of disease, so it would be brought back in the winter. The two parties disagreed and took the matter to the police station in the first district, who referred it to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for handling.

Murdered Male Corpse Discovered in a Creek on Zhongshan Road

An unidentified male corpse was found murdered in a small creek on Zhongshan Road, behind Datong University. The corpse was about twenty years old, dressed in a long feather gauze gown. His hands and feet were tied behind his back with a belt, and a silk ribbon was wrapped around his neck several times. A large stone was placed on his body. The police were notified and ordered the local constable to report to the local court for an inspection. Prosecutor Yang and others arrived at the scene and confirmed that the man had been strangled to death. They ordered the body to be collected and prepared for burial, and the case to be investigated.

Laborer Dies After Falling into River

At 10:30 a.m. the day before yesterday, a Victoria tugboat was unloading cargo from the Empress of Canada steamer at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong. A porter named Xu Yongqing, 22 years old, from Shaoxing, jumped onto the Empress of Canada steamer but accidentally fell into the river. Despite 50 minutes of searching, his body was recovered, but he was already dead. The incident was reported to the water police station, and detective Deng Jiagen took the body to the Lifesaving Bureau. Yesterday, they reported the incident to the local court for an inspection. Prosecutor Wu and others arrived at the scene and confirmed the death. They ordered the family to collect the body for burial.

Male Corpse Found Hanged from Evergreen Tree

An unidentified male corpse was discovered hanging from an evergreen tree in a cemetery near the Shanghai West Dapu Bridge railway line yesterday morning. He was believed to have committed suicide there the night before. The corpse was about thirty years old, dressed in a white cloth shirt and pants, white socks, and black shoes. The constable of the fifteenth district, Gu Zhonglian, reported the incident to the local court. Prosecutor Wu and others arrived at the scene, examined the body, took photographs, and ordered it to be collected for burial, awaiting family identification.

Prisoner Returns Home to a Completely Different Scene: House Appears Long Uninhabited; Wife Also Flees in the Interim

Liu Jingui, a 35-year-old resident of Kangli Number 15, Yangjiadu, outside Dadongmen in the Nanshi district and a native of Rugao, worked as a laborer at various docks. Last month, he was arrested and detained for two weeks in connection with a certain case. He was released yesterday and went home. However, upon returning home, he found that the tables and chairs inside were covered in dust, and the floor was extremely dirty, as if no one had lived there for a long time. He became suspicious and questioned his wife, Zhang, but she was evasive. He secretly inquired with his neighbors and learned that after he was detained, Zhang had left alone and had not been seen returning home. Liu was even more furious and questioned Zhang further. Zhang then claimed that she had been staying at the home of Chen Liu, a fellow villager, at Number 38 Qinglong Bridge. Liu did not believe her and forced her to go to Chen Liu's place to confront her and reveal the truth. Chen Liu, seeing that Liu had brought his wife with him, knew that something was amiss and used a trick to lure Liu away. She whispered to Liu, saying that she had two secret words to tell him and asked him to come upstairs to talk. Liu believed her and went upstairs with Liu. However, Zhang remained downstairs. After the two went upstairs, Liu whispered to Liu, "Your wife has indeed been staying at my place for several nights, but there is nothing else." She then asked him to go downstairs. Liu was suspicious of her strange behavior and quickly went downstairs to check on his wife, but she had already disappeared. He chased after her but could not find her. Liu then realized that Liu had conspired with his wife. He grabbed her and handed her over to Liu Bingrong, a guard at the 31st watch post, who took her to the first sub-district police station for investigation.

Business of the Gonghe Steamer Increases

Since the new comprador Chen Bonian took office, the British Jardine Matheson's Gonghe steamer has been making improvements, and its business has been thriving. The number of passengers has been increasing daily. The steamer arrived in Shanghai from Hankou yesterday and is docked at the Huashun Wharf. It is scheduled to depart for Hankou tonight.

Automobile Wheel Runs Over Child's Neck, Neck Severed and Brain Matter Flows Out, Resulting in Instant Death

Jin Gen, a five-year-old son of Cao Wu, a resident of Connaught Road in western Shanghai, went out to buy candy at 9 a.m. yesterday. As he was leaving the house, a truck from the Far Eastern Automobile Company carrying mud ran over him, severing his neck and causing brain matter to flow out. A police officer arrested the driver, Gu Wanhua, and took him along with the boy's mother to the sixth district police station. Because the child was severely injured, they were sent to the local court. However, the child died en route. Therefore, the body was also taken to the court. Prosecutor Wu conducted an examination and ordered the defendant to be detained. The body was released to his mother for burial, pending further investigation.

Burglary in Xuzhen, Pudong: Gang of Thieves in Gray Uniforms Armed with Guns and Cannons Abduct Shop Employees and Neighbors

At around 9 p.m. on the 10th, a gang of more than ten thieves, dressed in gray uniforms and armed with box cannons and handguns, raided two shops, Xia Changsheng and Wang Tongchang, in Xuzhen, Chuansha, Pudong. The total loss was about 300 yuan. Zhou Tulin, who was quite strong, used weapons to resist the thieves but was shot and wounded. The thieves, finding little cash, mistook two employees of Xia Changsheng as shop owners and abducted them. Chen Amao, who also resisted the thieves along with Zhou Tulin, was also taken away. It is rumored that the thieves headed northeast towards the coast and left by boat. The fate of the three kidnapped victims is currently unknown.

Robber Xia San Sentenced to Five Years in Prison

Guo Hongqing, a resident of Number 14 Jincheng Lane, Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, sent his employee Ji Asan with 74 yuan in cash to a cigarette paper shop at Number 295 Avenue Edward VII to exchange for small change at the end of last month. The robber Xia San and the fugitive Han Tingru saw this and planned a robbery. They pulled out a handgun and threatened Ji Asan, taking the cash. Li Dasheng shouted for help, and a police officer arrived and apprehended Xia. He was taken to the French Concession Court yesterday for investigation. The plaintiff, Guo Hongqing, described the robbery. Xia San confessed that Han Tingru, who is still at large, had proposed the robbery. The French and Chinese judges sentenced Xia to five years in a Western prison and ordered him to be permanently expelled from the French Concession after serving his sentence.

Illegal Sale of Red Pills Results in Fine

Police detectives discovered that Gu Adi, of Number 15 Yide Lane, Vegetable Market Street, was illegally selling red pills, violating the prohibition order. They raided his home and confiscated hundreds of red pills and over ten silver yuan in sales proceeds. He was taken to the French Concession Court yesterday for investigation. The police chief reported the situation and presented the red pills as evidence. Gu Adi admitted to illegally selling red pills. The French and Chinese judges fined Gu 300 yuan, which was to be confiscated. The confiscated red pills and silver yuan were also confiscated.

Xu Guanfu Dies Suddenly, Cause of Death Unknown, Wife Unwilling to Collect Body

Xu Guanfu, a 33-year-old native of Haimen, collapsed suddenly near Yuyuan Road and Yidingpan Road at 10 p.m. the night before last. He stood up and walked a few steps, but a foreign male and female couple and an Indian police officer from the 494 store saw him and knew that he was suffering from a sudden illness. The police officer hired a car to take him to the police station, intending to send him to the hospital. However, he died on the way. His body was taken to the Faelun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the incident was reported to the Special District Local Court, and Prosecutor Guo was appointed to inspect the body. The cause of death was unknown, and Xu's wife, Xu Lu, was unwilling to sign for the collection of the body, saying that she had telegraphed her hometown and asked the deceased's parents to come to Shanghai, and they would arrive soon. Prosecutor Guo ordered a forensic examination to be performed. The hearing was scheduled to continue on Saturday.

Publication of Pictorial Map of China

Mr. Kia Khoff, a Russian scholar with many talents, has traveled extensively throughout China in recent years. He has visited remote areas in Guizhou, Yunnan, Sichuan, Fujian, Guangdong, Gansu, Shaanxi, Tibet, and Qinghai that other scholars have not reached. He lived in the heart of Miao territory for two years, studying the customs of the Miao people in Yunnan and Guizhou and is proficient in the languages of the Miao, Yao, Li, and other ethnic groups. He has climbed mountains, crossed rivers, and traversed forests, and has been captured by bandits several times, but he has persevered. Mr. Kia is also skilled in photography and has taken photographs of the unique features of each place he has visited. Mr. Kia has created a pictorial map of the Republic of China, featuring the shapes of the country and figures of the people, using natural colors. The map clearly depicts the characteristics of different ethnic groups, local customs, the direction of mountain ranges, the flow of rivers and lakes, the elevation of the terrain, the condition of the oceans, the growth of plants, the breeding of animals, the buried minerals, land and sea transportation routes, seaports, and ancient architectural relics. The map is highly detailed and can enhance the interest of those studying geography. It is also suitable for use in schools. The map has been approved by the Department of Education of the Special Region of Eastern Provinces for use in schools and has been reviewed and approved by the Geography Research Association of the Harbin Oriental Languages and Business University and the Harbin Normal University. The publisher is the Harbin Northern Commercial Company Yao Xun, and the place of publication is the Publishing Department of the Northern Commercial Company, Number 16 Shangpu Street, Daoli District, Harbin, telephone number 4107.

The Xujiahui Observatory forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday that the weather in the Yangtze River basin and its north would be cloudy. A low-pressure system coming from northern Vietnam and Tonkin would move northeast or north-northeast. There would be a major cyclone over Kyushu and the southern Japanese coast. Special Item: The Call of the Overseas Chinese in Mexicali

The Cali Chinese Association in Mexicali published a call for help for unemployed and starving overseas Chinese, stating in the first paragraph that our overseas Chinese are under the economic oppression of foreigners. Our great rights have been lost, causing national economy and people's livelihood to be in great difficulty. Overseas Chinese have climbed mountains and sailed the seas, leaving their footprints all over the world to seek a living. They are steadfast, hardworking, thrifty, and hard-working. The statement continues that twenty years ago, the land was all wilderness, with few inhabitants. The overseas Chinese cleared the land and cultivated the fields, creating today's fertile and prosperous situation. This was all made from the sweat and blood of the overseas Chinese. How could there be such a new atmosphere without them? However, the Mexicans have various oppressive regulations. The most intense anti-Chinese sentiment is in the city of Mexicali. The cruelest anti-Chinese oppressive regulation is in Mexicali. Mexicali is mainly agricultural, and agriculture is mainly invested by Americans. Although the Mexicans know that the various industries of the overseas Chinese are struggling to survive, they show no pity. They force Chinese businessmen to increase the number of Mexican workers they hire; otherwise, they will seal the shops, detain people, and demand money. The labor party creates disturbances first, and the government encourages them later. The oppression is increasing daily and is unbearable

Bengbu 90

Joint Suppression of Bandits at Sanjue Temple. The area bordering Shouxian, Hefei, and Lu'an counties in northern Anhui has always been a hotbed of banditry. Despite repeated military campaigns, the bandits have not been completely eradicated. Recently, bandit activity has resurfaced in the vicinity of Sanjue Temple, with the bandit gang led by Zhang Zibin rampaging and causing great harm. Zhang Xiangkun, the county magistrate of Shouxian, and Quan Liting, the captain of the Fourth Brigade of the Lu'an Security Corps, each led their troops in a fierce pincer movement at the beginning of this month. The bandits, unable to resist, fled southeast. Subsequently, they were intercepted by the Security Corps stationed at Zaoshudian and fled into Hefei County. Upon receiving a report, the 270th Regiment of the 46th Division stationed in Hefei, led by Regiment Commander Hu, immediately led their troops to engage them head-on. Over a hundred bandits were killed at the time, greatly weakening the bandit force. Zhang Xiangkun then led his troops to encircle and suppress the bandits in the direction of Maji, while Quan Liting led his troops to advance on Wangji and Moziawan. The bandit gang has been surrounded and should be annihilated soon.

Educational News

Discussion

Should "Bird and Animal Language" Readings Be Abolished? ㈡ Chen Heqin 91

(B) I also saw a comical short film last week that could serve as a reference for us. This film is called "Animal Concert". Before the concert, many animals dressed in clothes, wearing glasses, and riding various means of transportation, came to attend this grand concert. Some rode in airships, "zhā: zhā::" flying down from the sky, some rode in cars, "wū: wū::" driving down from the bridge, some rode in trains, "gōng: gōng::" rushing from afar, and some rode in carriages, "dé: dé::" running from the street. All kinds of sights were very lively.

The program was quite interesting when the concert started. Suddenly, three or four frog girls, holding hands, opened their mouths, danced and sang. Suddenly, five or six mouse ladies, cocking their tails, raised their heads and sang with great enthusiasm, singing very well. Suddenly, a white cat gentleman, hanging his body, dangling his tail, played the piano with both hands, his eyes sometimes big and sometimes small, full of spirit. At that time, yellow dogs, roosters, crows... some played copper drums, some played xylophones... shouting and jumping, each offering their own talent. Sometimes it was like this, sometimes like that, for about ten minutes. After this film was shown, the whole audience applauded spontaneously. This kind of "Animal Concert" is purely a story in bird and animal language, and this kind of story is not only popular with children, but also very welcome to adults.

(5) In fact, readings in bird and animal language are very popular in Europe and America. I don't know what bad influence those European and American children have received from reading and listening to these readings. I will now talk about my own experience. My children can be said to like readings in bird and animal language very much. Not only ordinary readings in bird and animal language, but also very supernatural materials, such as Journey to the West, Erlang God capturing Sun Wukong, Investiture of the Gods, etc., are very much liked to listen to and watch.

Sometimes after I read it or they watched it themselves, I would ask them, "Is this true? Is there really a Sun Wukong? Can he really somersault 108,000 miles?" They all replied, "No, it's not possible." Sometimes they even replied, "This is a story, just telling it." I asked them again, "Since these stories are fake, why do you still like to listen to them?" They replied, "It's fun."

From this point of view, these recreational readings for children really do not have much hindrance to young children.

In conclusion, children, especially those under the age of seven or eight, like to listen to, watch, and perform readings in bird and animal language. How much harm does this kind of reading really do? It can be said to be very, very little. When they watch it, they only think it's fun and don't really believe it.

As for this kind of reading in bird and animal language, it is often told to children or shown to children, which of course has a kind of danger. This danger is the same as what children usually need, like "breastfeeding".

We all know that milk is a very good nutrient, and children cannot survive without it. However, if he is still breastfeeding after the age of one and a half, and does not eat anything else, then although he will not be in any danger, he will suffer losses. We should slowly give him some other things to eat. Readings in bird and animal language are somewhat similar to breastfeeding. Young children like to listen to stories in bird and animal language very much. I am afraid that at that time, we can only tell them those stories and write those readings for them, just like children under one year old can only be fed milk. When they grow up, they should eat less milk, and they should tell and watch less readings in bird and animal language, and show them more other readings. But we must never say that milk is a bad thing and cannot be given to him to eat.

Finally, I want to solemnly declare that readings in bird and animal language have their own considerable position and value. We adults have no right to deprive children of what they need, just like we deprive children of the right to breastfeed.

However, when children grow up, we should provide them with other materials to read, just like giving them other nutrients to eat after they have eaten milk.

Now, in our country, adult children's readings are still those kinds of bird and animal language and various supernatural stories, just like adult children still have to eat milk all day long. How can children be strong? We should try our best to compile various scientific stories to enrich his experience and arouse his interest.

I want to add that the various supernatural novels and martial arts novels that are currently published in bookstores are really not in line with children's psychology, and also contain a kind of misleading meaning. They even sell ridiculous and absurd readings that cause terror, such as various rabbit stories, etc. It is best not to show these stories to children. (End)

Important News

Yi Enbo Assumes Office as Director of Anhui Department of Education 92

Cheng Tianfang, the Director of the Anhui Department of Education, has served for more than two years and has an outstanding reputation. He left Anhui with his family in February of this year and firmly resigned to the central government. Various parties tried to persuade him to stay, but to no avail. The central government once announced Li Zhonggong, but he also firmly declined. For several months, the department's affairs have been handled by Secretary Li Zhongxiang, who, in addition to maintaining the status quo, has tried his best to increase the budget and handle the review and examination matters. Recently, the provincial government publicly recommended Provincial Committee Member Yi Enbo to concurrently serve as Director of the Department of Education. Yi took office on the morning of June 8th at 11:00 AM. After the handover was completed, the original Secretary Li Zhongxiang, Section Chief Chen Yingkun, Chen Xifang, and others all resigned. Yi tried to persuade them to stay, but to no avail. He then convened a meeting of department staff in the auditorium, saying that Director Cheng's past achievements were very good, and although he had been in education (Yi had served as Acting Director of Education in Shandong), it had been many years and he no longer had much interest. This time, the provincial government strongly recommended him, so he had to temporarily serve concurrently. He hoped that all department staff would continue to work diligently as in the past, except for those who had firmly resigned.

Ministry of Education Approves Zhejiang Education Association's Request 93

Director Zhang of the Department of Education Retained

Nanjing, 11th Telegram. The Zhejiang Provincial No. 2, No. 6, and No. 10 Middle School Faculty and Staff Associations, believing that Director Zhang Daofan of the Department of Education was determined to resign, telegraphed the Ministry of Education to quickly select a replacement to maintain education. The Ministry of Education replied, "Zhang Daofan's request to resign has been discussed and resolved by the State Council to retain him. The province's arrears in educational funding have also been referred by this Ministry to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to find ways to raise funds. The appointment of the Director is the central government's own prerogative. The requests of the said members are not appropriate and must be notified."

Special discussions will be held on appropriate measures to urge the authorities to pay attention.

Overseas School Diplomas Should Be Verified by the Consulate 95

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to all overseas consuls that overseas Chinese school diplomas should be verified and stamped by the consulate in the future. The case was based on the presentation by the Consulate General in Kobe of fifteen graduation certificates of students such as Chen Zongqi of the Kobe Overseas Chinese Tongwen School, requesting verification and return. The Ministry found that matters concerning overseas Chinese education administration have been clearly stipulated to be managed by the consulate. The verification of overseas Chinese school student diplomas falls within the scope of overseas Chinese education administration and should be handled by the consulate without the need to submit it to the Ministry. In addition to instructing the Consulate General in Kobe, this order is to be followed and communicated.

Graduates from Northeast China Visit Tianjin 96

Tianjin, 11th Telegram. Liu Xianzhu, a professor in the Department of Mechanical Engineering at Northeast University, arrived in Tianjin on the morning of the 10th with eighteen graduates. They are scheduled to visit various factories on the 11th, various universities on the 12th, and Ping and Changxindian on the 13th. Liu said that there is a shortage of technical personnel in various fields in Northeast China. The graduates of this year have all accepted employment from the arsenal and the Shenhai Railway.

Municipal Bureau of Education Investigates Primary and Secondary School Graduates 97

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, in order to provide guidance on further education and employment for graduates, ordered the city's private primary and secondary schools, stating, "It is appropriate to have guidance for graduates' further education and employment so as to suit their personality. Now, three categories of graduate surveys are issued. The first category should be filled out and submitted to the bureau for verification within one week for statistics. Another graduate voluntary survey form should be filled out by each student, stored for verification, etc."

Meeting of the Party Education Inspection Committee of the First District Party Headquarters 99

The Party Doctrine and Education Inspection Committee of the First District Party Headquarters of this city held its second meeting at the District Party Headquarters meeting room at 6:00 PM last night. The attendees were Zhou Fulu, Chen Weiyi, Lu Chongming, Ye Daolin, Fu Depei, Ye Guanqian, Xu Wanmei, and others, seven in total. Ye Guanqian chaired the meeting, and Xu Wanmei recorded the minutes. After the chairman reported on the progress and the status of the Party Doctrine courses received from various schools, the following motions were discussed, 1. How to assign inspections. "Resolved" that the chairman will report the school names and each committee member will be assigned an equal number of schools. 2. Setting the end date for inspections. "Resolved" that it must be completed before the 25th of this month. 3. How should the schools handle the submission of Party Doctrine timetable. "Resolved" that the inspection committee members will go to inspect at any time. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Time: 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM

Since the Third District Party Headquarters of this city began recruiting students for its People's School, enrollment has been exceptionally enthusiastic, with most being shop apprentices and out-of-school girls, aged fourteen and above. Shanghai Middle School Relief for the Shaanxi Famine 101

The faculty, staff, and students of Shanghai Middle School in this city expressed deep sympathy for the suffering of the Shaanxi famine. Previously, Chaizhao from the Relief Association went to the school to give a speech and showed a film of the disaster area, which moved the teachers and students even more. They each generously donated money for disaster relief. By the end of May, a total of 234.1 yuan had been raised and forwarded to the Shaanxi Disaster Relief Committee by the China Relief Society.

This is of utmost importance, etc. Upon receipt of this, it is found that the said member should take the examination and certification, and the forms to be filled out were issued in the past. In accordance with the previous order, this order is issued again to urge you to register by the deadline so that it can be sent to the department for review without delay. This is of utmost importance, etc."

Dr. Liu Xingchen to Return Home 105

Liu Xingchen is a native of Taixian, Jiangsu Province, and a Bachelor of Arts from Fudan University. He has served as a social science teacher at Shanghai Middle School and Pudong Middle School in Jiangsu Province. In the winter of the 17th year, he went to France to study, studying economics with great understanding. He has a special interest in monetary issues and has now obtained a doctorate in economics. His dissertation, titled "The Problem of Silver Depreciation and Its Remedial Methods," was praised by Professor You Deqi. He is now inspecting the economic situation in England and Germany, and will return to China by the Trans-Siberian Railway soon. It is also reported that Liu Junzhi and Shen Qi Jun have also obtained doctorates in economics. Liu's dissertation is titled "The Problem of China's Foreign Trade." Shen Jun plans to stay in France for several more months to conduct further research on political science with a certain professor before returning home.

Sports

Shaanxi Female Athlete Sets National Shot Put Record 106

The Shaanxi Provincial Capital Middle and Primary School Joint Sports Meet was held from May 29th to 21st for three days of track and field events. It was found that the women's shot put result in this sports meet broke the national record. The athlete was Ms. Yu Zhen of the First Women's Normal School, who set a new record of 8.35 meters for throwing an eight-pound shot put, which is 51 cm more than the record of 7.84 meters set by Ms. He Zhenkun of Liaoning in the women's shot put at last year's National Games.

Ma Ling Challenges China 107

Proposes Track and Field Confrontation After Being Unwilling to Accept Defeat

Decision on Whether to Hold It Will Be Made in the Next Few Days

Shang Weikai, the sports instructor of the US Marine Corps, wrote to Shen Siliang, the honorary chief of the All-China Athletic Association, proposing a track and field confrontation between Ma Ling and China. Before the International Games, Ma Ling and Jiangnan held a confrontation once, and Ma Ling won with 74 to 70. In the International Games, the United States lost with 104 points to 150 points. Most of the American team's organization was composed of Ma City athletes, and most of the Chinese team members were also from Jiangnan. Therefore, Ma Ling is unwilling to accept defeat and has the ambition to compete again. According to Shen Siliang, this move is very interesting, but most of the Chinese team members are students and are busy preparing for the big exam, which may be difficult. He will try his best to make it happen, and a decision on whether to hold it will be made in the next few days.

Postponement of This Year's Shanghai Middle School Sports Federation Games 108

It has been decided to hold it in the next semester

The 3rd Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation Games were originally scheduled to be held at the China Athletics Field today and tomorrow. Now, because the weather is hot and the schools are all busy preparing for the big exam, the committee has decided to postpone it and reschedule it for the next semester.

Recent News from the Municipal Stadium Tennis Club 109

The report on the third amateur tennis competition at the Municipal Stadium has been closed for a long time, and the start date is not far away. It is learned that the field will convert the southern half of the soccer field into six tennis courts during the tennis season to facilitate public training. Its original three tennis courts will be used for tennis competition and member practice to avoid mixing and to observe the level of the members. The levels can be observed to ensure fairness when they are assigned to groups in the future. It is also said that a small number of members of the association have not yet completed the registration procedures and must complete them before the 20th of this month, otherwise they will be invalid.
